         <h2 class="h2-mktg d-inline-block text-gradient-mint-blue">Frequently asked questions</h2> 
         <div class="my-6"> 
          <h3 class="h5-mktg color-text-white mb-2">Are prices listed only in US dollars?</h3> 
          <p class="f3 text-gray-light-mktg"> Yes, all prices shown are in US dollars. </p> 
         </div> 
         <div class="my-6"> 
          <h3 class="h5-mktg color-text-white mb-2">What types of accounts can I have on GitHub?</h3> 
          <p class="f3 text-gray-light-mktg"> GitHub offers personal user accounts, as well as organization and enterprise accounts. </p> 
          <p class="h6-mktg"> <a href="https://docs.github.com/en/github/getting-started-with-github/types-of-github-accounts" class="btn-mktg btn-invisible-mktg Bump-link color-text-white text-underline" data-hydro-click="{&quot;event_type&quot;:&quot;analytics.event&quot;,&quot;payload&quot;:{&quot;category&quot;:&quot;FAQ&quot;,&quot;action&quot;:&quot;click to learn more about each type of account&quot;,&quot;label&quot;:&quot;ref_page:/pricing;ref_cta:type of account;ref_loc:faq&quot;,&quot;originating_url&quot;:&quot;https://github.com/pricing&quot;,&quot;user_id&quot;:null}}" data-hydro-click-hmac="f3bf589064ed8f76b90c50f9d85db315a51bf1ff4bec5e2745a962e164e9bc52"> Learn more about each type of account <span class="Bump-link-symbol">?</span> </a> </p> 
         </div> 
         <div class="my-6"> 
          <h3 class="h5-mktg color-text-white mb-2">What are my organization뭩 deployment options?</h3> 
          <p class="f3 text-gray-light-mktg"> GitHub Enterprise comes with flexible deployment options at one per-seat price: cloud-hosted with Enterprise Cloud, self-hosted with Enterprise Server, or a hybrid of both. </p> 
          <p class="h6-mktg"> <a href="https://docs.github.com/en/github/getting-started-with-github/githubs-products#github-enterprise" class="btn-mktg btn-invisible-mktg Bump-link color-text-white text-underline" data-hydro-click="{&quot;event_type&quot;:&quot;analytics.event&quot;,&quot;payload&quot;:{&quot;category&quot;:&quot;FAQ&quot;,&quot;action&quot;:&quot;click to learn more about GitHub Enterprise&quot;,&quot;label&quot;:&quot;ref_page:/pricing;ref_cta:GitHub Enterprise;ref_loc:faq&quot;,&quot;originating_url&quot;:&quot;https://github.com/pricing&quot;,&quot;user_id&quot;:null}}" data-hydro-click-hmac="e4d1e357998aae808e5df23dd05f6ff6db376c3d40f6e1d08ef7e800572e1459"> Learn more about GitHub Enterprise <span class="Bump-link-symbol">?</span> </a> </p> 
         </div> 
         <div class="my-6"> 
          <h3 class="h5-mktg color-text-white mb-2">Which plans include access to GitHub Actions and Packages?</h3> 
          <p class="f3 text-gray-light-mktg"> GitHub Actions and Packages are free for public repositories and packages on all plans, while private repositories and packages receive a set amount of free minutes, storage, and data transfer depending on plan. </p> 
          <p class="h6-mktg d-md-flex"> <a href="/features/actions#pricing-details" class="no-wrap btn-mktg btn-invisible-mktg Bump-link color-text-white text-underline mr-5" data-hydro-click="{&quot;event_type&quot;:&quot;analytics.event&quot;,&quot;payload&quot;:{&quot;category&quot;:&quot;FAQ&quot;,&quot;action&quot;:&quot;click to learn more about billing for Actions&quot;,&quot;label&quot;:&quot;ref_page:/pricing;ref_cta:Billing for Actions;ref_loc:faq&quot;,&quot;originating_url&quot;:&quot;https://github.com/pricing&quot;,&quot;user_id&quot;:null}}" data-hydro-click-hmac="e8b93374e2c70790dbbbbc1e509f28bb4c0f24acaf87719870afc7da07a4154a"> Learn more about billing for Actions <span class="Bump-link-symbol">?</span> </a><br> <a href="/features/packages#pricing" class="no-wrap btn-mktg btn-invisible-mktg Bump-link color-text-white text-underline" data-hydro-click="{&quot;event_type&quot;:&quot;analytics.event&quot;,&quot;payload&quot;:{&quot;category&quot;:&quot;FAQ&quot;,&quot;action&quot;:&quot;click to learn more about billing for Packages&quot;,&quot;label&quot;:&quot;ref_page:/pricing;ref_cta:Billing for Packages;ref_loc:faq&quot;,&quot;originating_url&quot;:&quot;https://github.com/pricing&quot;,&quot;user_id&quot;:null}}" data-hydro-click-hmac="fe619cb904e8bf9ddef17f32cee3eefc5b1eefc8fd588ff4cf7875d7a7927464"> Learn more about billing for Packages <span class="Bump-link-symbol">?</span> </a> </p> 
         </div> 
         <div class="my-6"> 
          <h3 class="h5-mktg color-text-white mb-2">What if I want to change my plan?</h3> 
          <p class="f3 text-gray-light-mktg"> When you upgrade your plan, changes are applied immediately. When you downgrade your plan, changes are applied at the end of your current billing cycle. </p> 
          <p class="h6-mktg"> <a href="https://docs.github.com/en/github/setting-up-and-managing-billing-and-payments-on-github/how-does-upgrading-or-downgrading-affect-the-billing-process" class="btn-mktg btn-invisible-mktg Bump-link color-text-white text-underline" data-hydro-click="{&quot;event_type&quot;:&quot;analytics.event&quot;,&quot;payload&quot;:{&quot;category&quot;:&quot;FAQ&quot;,&quot;action&quot;:&quot;click to learn more about managing your plan&quot;,&quot;label&quot;:&quot;ref_page:/pricing;ref_cta:Managing Plan;ref_loc:faq&quot;,&quot;originating_url&quot;:&quot;https://github.com/pricing&quot;,&quot;user_id&quot;:null}}" data-hydro-click-hmac="b57357195bfa10654a2834245a266d453c737d274a39d2bd57a28c1d5efe1af7"> Learn more about managing your GitHub plan<span class="ml-1 Bump-link-symbol">?</span> </a> </p>
